elections; the\n// application is responsible for cleanup and recovery in this case.\ntype Storage interface {\n\t// TODO(tbg): split this into two interfaces, LogStorage and StateStorage.\n\n\t// For\n\t// example, common ways to do so are:\n\t//  - allocate the slice before returning it (safest option),\n\t//  - return a slice protected by Go full slice expression, which causes\n\t//  copying on appends (see MemoryStorage).\n\t//\n\t// Returns ErrCompacted if entry lo has been compacted, or ErrUnavailable if\n\t// encountered an unavailable entry in [lo, hi).\n\tEntries(lo, hi, maxSize uint64) ([]pb.Entry, error)\n\n\t// Term returns the term of entry i, which must be in the range\n\t// [FirstIndex()-1, LastIndex()]. The term of the entry before\n\t// FirstIndex is retained for matching purposes even though the\n\t// rest of that entry may not be available.\n\tTerm(i uint64) (uint64, error)\n\t// LastIndex returns the index of the last entry in the log.\n\tLastIndex() (uint64, error)\n\t// FirstIndex returns the index of the first log entry that is\n\t// possibly available via Entries (older entries have been incorporated\n\t// into the latest Snapshot; if storage only contains the dummy entry the\n\t// first log entry is not available).\n\tFirstIndex() (uint64, error)\n\t// Snapshot returns the most recent snapshot.\n\t// If snapshot is temporarily unavailable, it should return ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable,\n\t// so raft state machine could know that Storage needs some time to prepare\n\t// snapshot and call Snapshot later.\n\tSnapshot() (pb.Snapshot, error)\n}\n\ntype inMemStorageCallStats struct {\n\tinitialState, firstIndex, lastIndex, entries, term, snapshot int\n}\n\n// InMemoryRaftLog implements the Storage interface backed by an\n// in-memory array.\ntype InMemoryRaftLog struct {\n\t// Protects access to all fields. Most methods of InMemoryRaftLog are\n\t// run on the raft goroutine, but Append() is run on an application\n\t// goroutine.\n\tsync.Mutex\n\n\thardState pb.HardState\n\tsnapshot  pb.Snapshot\n\t// ents[i] has raft log position i+snapshot.Metadata.Index\n\tents []pb.Entry\n\n\tcallStats inMemStorageCallStats\n}\n\n// NewInMemoryRaftLog creates an empty InMemoryRaftLog.\nfunc NewInMemoryRaftLog() *InMemoryRaftLog {\n\treturn &InMemoryRaftLog{\n\t\t// When starting from scratch populate the list with a dummy entry at term zero.\n\t\tents: make([]pb.Entry, 1),\n\t}\n}\n\n// InitialState implements the Storage interface.\nfunc (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) InitialState() (pb.HardState, pb.ConfState, error) {\n\tms.callStats.initialState++\n\treturn ms.hardState, ms.snapshot.Metadata.ConfState, nil\n}\n\n// SetHardState saves the current HardState.\nfunc (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) SetHardState(st pb.HardState) error {\n\tms.Lock()\n\tdefer ms.Unlock()\n\tms.hardState = st\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// Entries implements the Storage interface.\nfunc (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) Entries(lo, hi, maxSize uint64) ([]pb.Entry, error) {\n\tms.Lock()\n\tdefer ms.Unlock()\n\tms.callStats.entries++\n\toffset := ms.ents[0].Index\n\tif lo <= offset {\n\t\treturn nil, ErrCompacted\n\t}\n\tif hi > ms.lastIndex()+1 {\n\t\tgetLogger().Panicf(\"entries' hi(%d) is out of bound lastindex(%d)\", hi, ms.lastIndex())\n\t}\n\t// only contains dummy entries.\n\tif len(ms.ents) == 1 {\n\t\treturn nil, ErrUnavailable\n\t}\n\n\tents := limitSize(ms.ents[lo-offset:hi-offset], entryEncodingSize(maxSize))\n\t// NB: use the full slice expression to limit what the caller can do with the\n\t// returned slice. For example, an append will reallocate and copy this slice\n\t// instead of corrupting the neighbouring ms.ents.\n\treturn ents[:len(ents):len(ents)], nil\n}\n\n// Term implements the Storage interface.\nfunc (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) Term(i uint64) (uint64, error) {\n\tms.Lock()\n\tdefer ms.Unlock()\n\tms.callStats.term++\n\toffset := ms.ents[0].Index\n\tif i < offset {\n\t\treturn 0, ErrCompacted\n\t}\n\tif int(i-offset) >= len(ms.ents) {\n\t\treturn 0, ErrUnavailable\n\t}\n\treturn ms.ents[i-offset].Term, nil\n}\n\n// LastIndex implements the Storage interface.\nfunc (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) LastIndex() (uint64, error) {\n\tms.Lock()\n\tdefer ms.Unlock()\n\tms.callStats.lastIndex++\n\treturn ms.lastIndex(), nil\n}\n\nfunc (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) lastIndex() uint64 {\n\treturn ms.ents[0].Index + uint64(len(ms.ents)) - 1\n}\n\n// FirstIndex implements the Storage interface.\nfunc (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) FirstIndex() (uint64, error) {\n\tms.Lock()\n\tdefer ms.Unlock()\n\tms.callStats.firstIndex++\n\treturn ms.firstIndex(), nil\n}\n\nfunc (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) firstIndex() uint64 {\n\treturn ms.ents[0].Index + 1\n}\n\n// Snapshot implements the Storage interface.\nfunc (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) Snapshot() (pb.Snapshot, error) {\n\tms.Lock()\n\tdefer ms.Unlock()\n\tms.callStats.snapshot++\n\treturn ms.snapshot, nil\n}\n\n// ApplySnapshot overwrites the contents of this Storage object with\n// those of the given snapshot.\nfunc (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) ApplySnapshot(snap pb.Snapshot) error {\n\tms.Lock()\n\tdefer ms.Unlock()\n\n\t//handle check for old snapshot being applied\n\tmsIndex := ms.snapshot.Metadata.Index\n\tsnapIndex := snap.Metadata.Index\n\t// During bootstrap, applications (e.g., etcd) may initialize only the\n\t// ConfState in the snapshot. In this case, both the snapshot index and\n\t// term are 0.\n\tif msIndex != 0 && msIndex >= snapIndex {\n\t\treturn ErrSnapOutOfDate\n\t}\n\n\tms.snapshot = snap\n\tms.ents = []pb.Entry{{Term: snap.Metadata.Term, Index: snap.Metadata.Index}}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// CreateSnapshot makes a snapshot which can be retrieved with Snapshot() and\n// can be used to reconstruct the state at that point.\n// If any configuration changes have been made since the last compaction,\n// the result of the last ApplyConfChange must be passed in.\nfunc (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) CreateSnapshot(i uint64, cs *pb.ConfState, data []byte) (pb.Snapshot, error) {\n\tms.Lock()\n\tdefer ms.Unlock()\n\tif i <= ms.snapshot.Metadata.Index {\n\t\treturn pb.Snapshot{}, ErrSnapOutOfDate\n\t}\n\n\toffset := ms.ents[0].Index\n\tif i > ms.lastIndex() {\n\t\tgetLogger().Panicf(\"snapshot %d is out of bound lastindex(%d)\", i, ms.lastIndex())\n\t}\n\n\tms.snapshot.Metadata.Index = i\n\tms.snapshot.Metadata.Term = ms.ents[i-offset].Term\n\tif cs != nil {\n\t\tms.snapshot.Metadata.ConfState = *cs\n\t}\n\tms.snapshot.Data = data\n\treturn ms.snapshot, nil\n}\n\n// Compact discards all log entries prior to compactIndex.\n// It is the application's responsibility to not attempt to compact an index\n// greater than raftLog.applied.\nfunc (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) Compact(compactIndex uint64) error {\n\tms.Lock()\n\tdefer ms.Unlock()\n\toffset := ms.ents[0].Index\n\tif compactIndex <= offset {\n\t\treturn ErrCompacted\n\t}\n\tif compactIndex > ms.lastIndex() {\n\t\tgetLogger().Panicf(\"compact %d is out of bound lastindex(%d)\", compactIndex, ms.lastIndex())\n\t}\n\n\ti := compactIndex - offset\n\t// NB: allocate a new slice instead of reusing the old ms.ents. Entries in\n\t// ms.ents are immutable, and can be referenced from outside InMemoryRaftLog\n\t// through slices returned by ms.Entries().\n\tents := make([]pb.Entry, 1, uint64(len(ms.ents))-i)\n\tents[0].Index = ms.ents[i].Index\n\tents[0].Term = ms.ents[i].Term\n\tents = append(ents, ms.ents[i+1:]...)\n\tms.ents = ents\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// Append the new entries to storage.\n// TODO (xiangli): ensure the entries are continuous and\n// entries[0].Index > ms.entries[0].Index\nfunc (ms *InMemoryRaftLog) Append(entries []pb.Entry) error {\n\tif len(entries) == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tms.Lock()\n\tdefer ms.Unlock()\n\n\tfirst := ms.firstIndex()\n\tlast := entries[0].Index + uint64(len(entries)) - ms.ents[0].Index\n\tswitch {\n\tcase uint64(len(ms.ents)) > offset:\n\t\t// NB: full slice expression protects ms.ents at index >= offset from\n\t\t// rewrites, as they may still be referenced from outside InMemoryRaftLog.\n\t\tms.ents = append(ms.ents[:offset:offset], entries...)\n\tcase uint64(len(ms.ents)) == offset:\n\t\tms.ents = append(ms.ents, entries...)\n\tdefault:\n\t\tgetLogger().Panicf(\"missing log entry [last: %d, append at: %d]\",\n\t\t\tms.lastIndex(), entries[0].Index)\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":64,"oldLines":7,"newStart":64,"newLines":7,"lines":["   // example, common ways to do so are:","   //  -
